RhinoVLA Technical Report

RhinoVLA 技术报告

Huixi Intelligence、 :、Chen Zhang、Chenyang Zhou、Guanglei Ding 等

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 ⭐ GitHub 开源

Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown strong potential for robotic manipulation, but real-time deployment on edge hardware remains challenging. In this work, we identify VLM visual and context tokens as a major source of deployment latency: for GEMM-dominated projection operators, computation grows linearly with the number of input tokens when model dimensions are fixed. Motivated by this observation, we propose RhinoVLA, a deployment-oriented VLA model co-designed with the Huixi R1 edge SoC. RhinoVLA adopts a token-efficient Qwen3-VL backbone and a continuous Action Expert, reducing the VLM-side token and computation burden while preserving pretrained multimodal capability. To support cross-robot learning, RhinoVLA further introduces a unified interface that combines View Registry, 72D physical state-action slot space, and robotinstance LoRA, allowing heterogeneous robot observations and action schemas to be aligned under a shared policy. On the deployment side, RhinoVLA is optimized through hardware-aware compilation, mixed-precision execution, and parallel visual encoding. Experiments show that RhinoVLA achieves downstream performance comparable to π0.5 at a similar parameter scale, while reaching 11.69 Hz end-to-end inference on Huixi R1, meeting the 10 Hz real-time closedloop control target. The project will be open-sourced at https://github.com/HuixiAI/RhinoVLA.

视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在机器人操作方面显示出强大的潜力，但在边缘硬件上的实时部署仍然具有挑战性。在这项工作中，我们将 VLM 视觉和上下文标记确定为部署延迟的主要来源：对于 GEMM 主导的投影算子，当模型维度固定时，计算量随着输入标记的数量线性增长。受这一观察的启发，我们提出了RhinoVLA，这是一种与汇熙R1边缘SoC共同设计的面向部署的VLA模型。 RhinoVLA 采用代币高效的 Qwen3-VL 主干和连续操作专家，减少了 VLM 端代币和计算负担，同时保留了预训练的多模式能力。为了支持跨机器人学习，RhinoVLA进一步引入了一个统一的接口，结合了ViewRegistry、72D物理状态动作槽空间和机器人实例LoRA，允许异构机器人观察和动作模式在共享策略下对齐。在部署方面，RhinoVLA 通过硬件感知编译、混合精度执行和并行视觉编码进行了优化。实验表明，RhinoVLA在相似的参数尺度下实现了与π0.5相当的下游性能，同时在慧喜R1上达到了11.69 Hz的端到端推理，满足10 Hz实时闭环控制目标。该项目将在 https://github.com/HuixiAI/RhinoVLA 开源。

AEGIS: A Backup Reflex for Physical AI

AEGIS：物理 AI 的后备反射

Josef Chen

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 暂无开源

Long-horizon robot manipulation tends to fail gradually: one bad step degrades the state, and the policy spirals into a basin from which it cannot recover. The failure is often visible before it happens. We introduce AEGIS (Activation-probe Early-warning, Gated Inference Switching), a selective escalation method that uses a lightweight probe on a weak policy's frozen activations to detect high-risk steps while there is still time to act. When the probe flags a step, control switches to a stronger separate policy, but only for the steps that need it. On LIBERO-Spatial, AEGIS recovers 10.1% of the trajectories the weak policy alone loses, versus 4.6% for budget-matched blind escalation and 5.1% for a random-trigger placebo. These gains are significant under one-sided exact paired McNemar tests with Holm-Bonferroni adjustment over three pre-registered contrasts: +5.4pp over blind escalation, p=8.5e-6; +5.0pp over random triggering, p=1.0e-4; paired-trajectory bootstrap CIs exclude zero. AEGIS activates the stronger policy on only 38% of steps, so the lever is timing rather than compute. The probe clears its precondition with an early-window AUROC of 0.764, 95% CI [0.70, 0.84], read from the weak-policy path over the first 30% of trajectory steps before any handoff. We pre-register the full analysis plan, including a conditional recovered-task-rate estimand and explicit kill criteria, and confirm the result on 700 common-random-number episodes per arm, with nA-fail=646.

长期的机器人操纵往往会逐渐失败：一步错误就会使国家退化，政策就会陷入无法恢复的深渊。故障通常在发生之前就可见。我们引入了 AEGIS（激活探测预警，门控推理切换），这是一种选择性升级方法，它对弱策略的冻结激活使用轻量级探测，以在仍有时间采取行动时检测高风险步骤。当探测器标记一个步骤时，控制会切换到更强大的单独策略，但仅适用于需要它的步骤。在 LIBERO-Spatial 上，AEGIS 恢复了仅弱政策损失的 10.1% 的轨迹，而预算匹配盲目升级的恢复率为 4.6%，随机触发安慰剂的恢复率为 5.1%。在对三个预先注册的对比进行 Holm-Bonferroni 调整的单边精确配对 McNemar 测试下，这些增益是显着的：+5.4pp 超过盲目升级，p=8.5e-6； +5.0pp 超过随机触发，p=1.0e-4；配对轨迹引导 CI 排除零。 AEGIS 仅在 38% 的步骤上激活更强的策略，因此杠杆是计时而不是计算。该探测器清除了其前提条件，早期窗口 AUROC 为 0.764，95% CI [0.70, 0.84]，从任何切换之前的前 30% 轨迹步骤的弱策略路径中读取。我们预先注册了完整的分析计划，包括条件恢复任务率估计值和明确的杀死标准，并在每组 700 个常见随机数事件上确认结果，其中 nA-fail=646。

Cubic Hermite Lattice Structures

立方埃尔米特晶格结构

Yaonaiming Zhao、Yuntao Ma、Guoyue Luo、Qiang Zou

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 暂无开源

Lattice structures are of growing importance in additive manufacturing, where complex internal geometries are increasingly required for lightweight, high surface-to-volume ratios, multifunctionality, and other superior mechanical properties. Conventional lattice modeling methods typically represent struts with simple primitives, such as cylinders or cones, limiting geometric diversity and the design space. Although recent efforts have increased strut-shape complexity to address this issue, they often do so at the expense of computational efficiency and modeling robustness. As a result, achieving both rich geometric expressiveness and efficient computation remains a challenging problem. In this paper, we present an implicit modeling method that expands the design and optimization space of lattice structures while preserving the modeling robustness and efficiency of implicit representations. In our method, each strut is defined as a convolution surface over a skeletal graph, and its profile shape is controlled by a cubic Hermite curve. By exploiting the polynomial structure of both the convolution kernel and the cubic Hermite curve-controlled profile, we derive analytical expressions for efficient field evaluation, avoiding costly and unstable numerical computation. Four case studies have been conducted to validate the proposed method in terms of profile shape diversity, graded lattice modeling, as well as slicing robustness and efficiency.

晶格结构在增材制造中变得越来越重要，为了实现轻质、高表面积体积比、多功能性和其他卓越的机械性能，复杂的内部几何形状的需求越来越大。传统的晶格建模方法通常用简单的图元（例如圆柱体或圆锥体）来表示支柱，从而限制了几何多样性和设计空间。尽管最近的努力增加了支柱形状的复杂性来解决这个问题，但它们往往以牺牲计算效率和建模鲁棒性为代价。因此，同时实现丰富的几何表现力和高效的计算仍然是一个具有挑战性的问题。在本文中，我们提出了一种隐式建模方法，该方法扩展了晶格结构的设计和优化空间，同时保留了隐式表示的建模鲁棒性和效率。在我们的方法中，每个支柱被定义为骨架图上的卷积表面，其轮廓形状由三次埃尔米特曲线控制。通过利用卷积核和三次 Hermite 曲线控制轮廓的多项式结构，我们推导了有效场评估的解析表达式，避免了昂贵且不稳定的数值计算。我们进行了四个案例研究，以在轮廓形状多样性、分级晶格建模以及切片稳健性和效率方面验证所提出的方法。

Agentic Large Language Models for Automated Structural Analysis of 3D Frame Systems

用于 3D 框架系统自动结构分析的代理大语言模型

Ziheng Geng、Ian Franklin、Santiago Martinez、Jiachen Liu、Yunhe Zhao 等

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 暂无开源

Large language models (LLMs) have emerged as powerful foundation models with strong reasoning capabilities across domains. Beyond reactive text generation, agentic LLMs enable autonomous workflow execution through modular task decomposition and coordinated tool use. In structural engineering, recent efforts have developed agentic LLMs for automated analysis of plane frames. However, their extension to 3D frames remains underexplored due to challenges in irregular geometric representation, topological consistency, and long-horizon reasoning. This paper proposes an agentic LLM framework for automated structural analysis of 3D frames from natural language inputs. Irregular 3D frames are represented by projection onto a 2D plan, where orthogonal gridlines define spatial coordinates and a matrix of number of stories encodes vertical extrusion of each grid cell. Building on this representation, the framework establishes a multi-agent pipeline: a problem analysis agent parses input into structured JSON; a floor decomposition agent derives the spatial layout of each floor; the 3D geometry is assembled by node, girder, slab, and column agents; support and load agents assign boundary and loading conditions, and code translation agents generate executable SAP2000 script. Evaluated on ten representative 3D frames, the proposed framework achieves an average accuracy of 90% across repeated trials, demonstrating consistent and reliable performance.

大型语言模型（LLM）已成为强大的基础模型，具有强大的跨领域推理能力。除了反应式文本生成之外，代理法学硕士还可以通过模块化任务分解和协调工具使用来实现自主工作流程执行。在结构工程领域，最近的努力开发了用于平面框架自动分析的代理法学硕士。然而，由于不规则几何表示、拓扑一致性和长视野推理方面的挑战，它们对 3D 框架的扩展仍未得到充分探索。本文提出了一种代理法学硕士框架，用于对自然语言输入的 3D 框架进行自动结构分析。不规则的 3D 框架通过投影到 2D 平面上来表示，其中正交网格线定义空间坐标，故事数矩阵编码每个网格单元的垂直挤压。在此表示的基础上，该框架建立了一个多代理管道：问题分析代理将输入解析为结构化 JSON；楼层分解代理导出每层的空间布局； 3D 几何体由节点、梁、板和柱代理组装；支持和加载代理分配边界和加载条件，代码翻译代理生成可执行的 SAP2000 脚本。通过对 10 个代表性 3D 帧进行评估，所提出的框架在重复试验中实现了 90% 的平均准确度，表现出一致且可靠的性能。

On orbital stabilization of a circular motion primitive for a dynamic extension of the Dubins car model

关于杜宾斯汽车模型动态扩展的圆周运动基元的轨道稳定性

Artem Angelchev-Shiryaev、Pavel E. Aleshin、Anton S. Shiriaev、Pavel A. Shamanaev、Leonid B. Freidovich 等

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 暂无开源

This paper addresses orbital stabilization of a circular motion primitive for a dynamic extension of the Dubins car model within a transverse-linearization framework. We show that the corresponding transverse linearization is unstable and not stabilizable by linear state feedback. Therefore, the standard linearization-based approach to orbital stabilization cannot be applied directly. The main contribution is a set of explicit and verifiable conditions that characterize when a controller design based on transverse linearization remains applicable. These conditions rely on the specific structure of the dynamics in a neighborhood of the motion and on the use of non-standard transverse coordinates for controller design and analysis. Numerical simulations illustrate the proposed design procedure.

本文讨论了横向线性化框架内杜宾斯汽车模型动态扩展的圆周运动原语的轨道稳定性。我们表明，相应的横向线性化是不稳定的，并且不能通过线性状态反馈来稳定。因此，不能直接应用基于标准线性化的轨道稳定方法。主要贡献是一组明确且可验证的条件，这些条件表征基于横向线性化的控制器设计何时仍然适用。这些条件依赖于运动邻域中动力学的具体结构以及控制器设计和分析中非标准横向坐标的使用。数值模拟说明了所提出的设计过程。

2026-06-05

Skeletal-Anchored Dual Harmonics for Structured 3D Modeling

用于结构化 3D 建模的骨骼锚定双谐波

Zhentao Huang、Changhao Li、Ruizhen Hu、Hui Huang、Minglun Gong 等

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 暂无开源

We present Skeletal-Anchored Dual Harmonics (SADH), a novel 3D shape representation that tightly couples local surface geometry with internal meso-skeletal organization. SADH represents a shape as a collection of compact surface patches rooted on internal anchors optimized directly inside the object volume. Each patch is parameterized using a dual-channel spherical harmonic (SH) formulation, where one channel models local radial geometry while the other defines adaptive patch support through a generalized viewing cone. Unlike isotropic primitives such as medial spheres or Gaussian kernels, SH patches directly encode anisotropic local surface geometry together with adaptive spatial support, enabling compact representation of detailed and directionally varying surface regions. Starting from unorganized point clouds, SADH jointly optimizes surface geometry, anchor locations, patch orientations, and structural connectivity through a staged optimization process that progressively forms a coherent meso-skeletal structure. A geodesic anchor graph further preserves structural relationships between neighboring patches. Experiments on complex 3D shapes demonstrate that SADH achieves accurate surface reconstruction together with compact and coherent skeletal organization across a wide range of geometries.

我们提出了骨骼锚定双谐波 (SADH)，这是一种新颖的 3D 形状表示，它将局部表面几何形状与内部细观骨骼组织紧密耦合。 SADH 将形状表示为紧凑表面块的集合，这些表面块植根于直接在对象体积内优化的内部锚点。每个补丁都使用双通道球谐函数 (SH) 公式进行参数化，其中一个通道模拟局部径向几何形状，而另一个通道通过广义视锥定义自适应补丁支持。与中间球体或高斯核等各向同性基元不同，SH 补丁直接对各向异性局部表面几何图形与自适应空间支持一起进行编码，从而能够紧凑地表示详细且方向变化的表面区域。从无组织的点云开始，SADH 通过分阶段的优化过程联合优化表面几何形状、锚点位置、面片方向和结构连接性，逐步形成连贯的细观骨骼结构。测地线锚图进一步保留了相邻斑块之间的结构关系。对复杂 3D 形状的实验表明，SADH 可以在各种几何形状中实现精确的表面重建以及紧凑且连贯的骨骼组织。

Re-imagining ISO 26262 in the Age of Autonomous Vehicles: Enhancing Controllability through Transferability and Predictability

重新构想自动驾驶汽车时代的 ISO 26262：通过可转移性和可预测性增强可控性

Chaitanya Shinde、Hadi Hajieghrary、Paul Schmitt、Adam Shoemaker、Bodo Seifert 等

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 暂无开源

The ISO 26262 standard defines functional safety for road vehicles through risk assessments based on Severity, Exposure, and Controllability, grounded in a human-driven vehicle paradigm. In the context of autonomous vehicles (AVs), the absence of a human driver necessitates revisiting these principles. This paper decomposes the Controllability placeholder into two auditable evidence dimensions of ISO 26262 by introducing two measurable sub-concepts: Transferability and Predictability. Transferability extends Controllability to capture AV systems' ability to hand off control to dedicated fallback safety mechanisms, while Predictability captures how easily external agents can anticipate AV behavior. Predictability is formally defined from human-robot interaction-inspired principles, and a mathematical framework is provided to quantify it. A designed-versus-achievable gap is introduced to distinguish architectural fallback claims from scene-conditioned achievable fallback capability. The proposed metrics align with ISO 26262 and ISO/PAS 21448 (SOTIF), rendering fallback and interaction claims falsifiable and traceable across ODD slices. These dimensions complement rather than replace existing standards, and the enhancements preserve the structure of ISO 26262 while extending its applicability to driverless automated systems operating at SAE Levels 4 and 5.

ISO 26262 标准通过基于严重性、暴露性和可控性的风险评估来定义道路车辆的功能安全，并以人类驾驶车辆范例为基础。在自动驾驶汽车 (AV) 的背景下，由于没有人类驾驶员，因此有必要重新审视这些原则。本文通过引入两个可衡量的子概念：可转移性和可预测性，将可控性占位符分解为 ISO 26262 的两个可审计证据维度。可转移性扩展了可控性，以捕获 AV 系统将控制权移交给专用后备安全机制的能力，而可预测性则捕获外部代理预测 AV 行为的容易程度。可预测性是根据人机交互启发的原理正式定义的，并提供了一个数学框架来量化它。引入了设计与可实现的差距，以区分架构后备声明和场景条件可实现的后备功能。提议的指标与 ISO 26262 和 ISO/PAS 21448 (SOTIF) 保持一致，使回退和交互声明在 ODD 切片上可证伪且可追踪。这些尺寸补充而不是取代现有标准，增强功能保留了 ISO 26262 的结构，同时将其适用性扩展到在 SAE 4 级和 5 级运行的无人驾驶自动化系统。

AI Level of Detail: Distance-Aware ML Model Precision Selection for Real-Time Human Motion Prediction in Games

AI 细节级别：游戏中实时人体运动预测的距离感知 ML 模型精度选择

Mathew Varghese

论文页面 PDF HTML 版本 暂无开源

Modern game engines spend significant compute animating NPCs with learned motion models. This paper proposes AI Level of Detail (AI LOD), a framework in which machine learning inference precision is adapted based on the distance between each NPC and the player camera. The core idea mirrors classical geometry LOD: substitute a cheaper approximation where the difference is imperceptible. Here, the approximation is a lower-precision quantized machine learning model rather than a lower-polygon mesh. The contribution of this work is the AI LOD concept itself: that inference-time quantization can serve as the LOD axis for AI-driven character animation - and more broadly, for any AI-based runtime system where perceptual sensitivity varies with context. The convolutional sequence-to-sequence model of Li et al. is used as a representative example to demonstrate the concept, with its trained checkpoint exported into three ONNX Runtime variants (FP32, FP16, and INT8 per-tensor), intended to be routed by a distance-based selector at runtime. Evaluation on the CMU Mocap dataset provides initial evidence that each precision tier can be served at its assigned distance range with negligible perceptible degradation, supporting the broader premise that distance-aware ML model precision selection is a viable LOD strategy for AI-based character animation.

现代游戏引擎花费大量计算来通过学习的运动模型来制作 NPC 动画。本文提出了 AI 细节级别 (AI LOD)，这是一个框架，其中根据每个 NPC 与玩家相机之间的距离来调整机器学习推理精度。核心思想反映了经典几何 LOD：在差异难以察觉的情况下替换更便宜的近似值。这里，近似是一个较低精度的量化机器学习模型，而不是一个较低多边形的网格。 这项工作的贡献在于 AI LOD 概念本身：推理时间量化可以作为 AI 驱动的角色动画的 LOD 轴，更广泛地说，对于感知灵敏度随上下文而变化的任何基于 AI 的运行时系统。 Li 等人的卷积序列到序列模型。用作演示该概念的代表性示例，其经过训练的检查点导出为三个 ONNX 运行时变体（每个张量 FP32、FP16 和 INT8），旨在在运行时由基于距离的选择器进行路由。对 CMU Mocap 数据集的评估提供了初步证据，表明每个精度层都可以在其指定的距离范围内提供服务，且可察觉的退化可以忽略不计，这支持了更广泛的前提，即距离感知 ML 模型精度选择是基于 AI 的角色动画的可行 LOD 策略。
